<span style='color:blue;'>Experiment: ex_2

Author: James McArdle


This program performs symbolic regression using a simple genetic programming approach.


It reads input data from a binary file, generates mathematical expressions, evaluates them against the data, and evolves the expressions over multiple generations to find better fits.


- Input file:        ../50k_data/ps_data_50k.f32

- Tolerance:         0.025
- Cutoff Score:      100
- Max Floats:        1000
- Max Generations:   10
